## Page 2

林俊杰
Apache RocketMQ Committer, 聚得
师。从2017年起开始参与RocketMQ社区的工
作，雪任职甲骨文，OPPO，现为某头部上市公
司后台架构师，拥有11年中间件产品和大型业务
后台的双障景研发经历，对海量用户、高并发、
多地域容灾等架构设计拥有丰富经验，热表于债
术总结与加只分享。

## Page 4

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">   </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">本书以</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ 4.9.5 （</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">编写本书时最新的</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">4.x</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000"> 版本</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">为基</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">础</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">从</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000"> 的实际使用</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">原理剖析</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">大规模消息集群下企</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">业级落地的实践以及所面临的挑战</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">逐一由浅入深地进行讲解</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">全书分</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000"> 篇</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">共</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">16</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000"> 章</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">基础篇包含第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">1 ～4</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000"> 章</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">主要讲解</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">Apache</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000"> 入门以及如何掌握</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000"> 的基础使用</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">原理篇包含</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">5～12</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000"> 章</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">主要讲解了消费原理</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">负载均衡原理</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">顺序消息原理等核</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">心的</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000"> 部分</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">进阶篇包含第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">13 ～16</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000"> 章</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">主要讲解消息幂等</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">双</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">活设计等进阶为架构师必须掌握的内容</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">讲解过程中抛弃了传统的源码</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">解析这种较枯燥的手段</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">而是更多地利用以下方式帮助读者更快</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">更轻</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">松地接受</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000"> 的原理</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">通过近百张原创的手绘图</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">形象地</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">描述</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000"> 的运作过程</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">原理</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">；</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">通过与</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">Kafka、RabbitMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000"> 等</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">成熟的消息中间件产品做对比的方式</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">有助于读者对相关知识触类旁</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">通</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">举一反三</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">；</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">每章都有思考题</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">以便于读者总结思考所学内容</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">进行</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">灵活运用</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">随书附赠示意代码</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">获取方式见封底</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">本书适合对</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000"> 感兴趣的读者阅读</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">本书的内容能帮</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">助读者快速地从入门到精通</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">并借助书中所总结的实践经验</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">在工作中</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">更好地设计出高并发</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">高可用的后台系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">支撑互联网业务的高速</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">发展</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">。</span>

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">  </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">机</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">工</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">官</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">博</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">：weibo. com / cmp1952</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">  </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">金</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">书</span>

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">  </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">机工教育服务网</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">：www. cmpedu. com</span>

## Page 5

<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">随着移动互联网的充分发展，各种新技术层出不穷，只有优秀的技术才能经得起行业</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">的考验。而消息中间件是后台技术栈中绕不开的一个技术组件，其是应对海量用户、高并</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">发、高可靠的架构挑战的超级利器。</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 正是这样一款足够优秀的消息中间</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">件产品。</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 脱胎于阿里巴巴的“双十一”，经过多年“双十一”洪峰流量</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">的考验，其性能、稳定性已经得到证明，而后广泛应用于多个大型的互联网公司，如滴</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">滴、微众银行等，已经成为国内最优秀、最受欢迎的消息中间件之一。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">经过多年的发展，介绍</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 的书籍、文章已不少。读者可以借助这些优秀的书</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">籍、文章去学习</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 的使用，去了解源码的实现。然而一些书籍或者博客文章大多</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">基于源码解读的方式展开，这种方式对于深入学习确实很有益处，但是学习难度较大且</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">较为枯燥，使初学者产生畏难情绪。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">笔者于</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">2016</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 年因公司项目需要，开始学习并使用</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">，之后有幸认识</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">了社区中多位优秀的贡献者，从而也成为</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 的贡献者之一。之后在知乎、</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">博客等平台撰写了多篇介绍</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 原理的文章，因文章的风格深入浅出、图文并茂，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">得到</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 作者的赞赏。本着希望优秀的</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 的原理能被更多人</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">认识与学习，遂产生了系统地撰写一本介绍</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 原理的书籍的想法。之后有</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">幸结识到机械工业出版社的编辑，在他们的帮助和鼓励下，历时两年完成了本书的撰写。</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">本书的宗旨是让读者能轻松掌握</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 的原理、最佳实践，所以放弃了贴</span>

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">.</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000">Ⅲ</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000"> </span>

## Page 6

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZBIAOYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef"> 进阶之路</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">源码、贴示意代码的传统方式。而是大量采取图表说明的方式进行展开。希望通过这种方</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">式能帮助读者利用地铁上、睡觉前等碎片时间轻松理解</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 的原理并掌握其</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">优秀的实践。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">同时，本书的结构采取由浅入深的方式。全书分基础篇、原理篇、进阶篇。基础篇讲</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">解</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 的基础使用及一些最佳实践的总结。原理篇按模块点深入讲解</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 的核心设计，是</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 设计中最精华的部分，通过此部分的学习，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">读者将深入掌握别人需要阅读源码才能掌握的优秀设计。进阶篇则是笔者在多年大型互</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">联网项目的实践中遇到的一些高级话题、难题，能帮助不少开发人员成为优秀架构师。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">在内容上，本书采取类比讲解的方式去展开一些知识点。例如讲解顺序消息的章节同</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">时也会介绍</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Kafka</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 的实现、在讲解事务消息的章节也会介绍分布式事务的通用解决方案，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">通过这种方式很容易引导读者思考和联想，使得知识的掌握更为轻松。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">类似课堂的学习一样，每一章的结束都会留一道或数道思考题，以便进一步加深对知</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">识的掌握与理解。</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">希望学习</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 的人员。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">已经有</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 的使用经验，希望能进一步了解其原理、掌握最佳实践的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">人员。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">从事消息中间件或者分布式系统研发的开发人员。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">企业消息中间件的维护、运维人员。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 社区贡献者。</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">本书内容虽然已深入到</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 的核心原理部分，但是内容的展开会采取循</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">序渐进的方式进行。本书分三大部分。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 部分是基础篇，包含第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">1 ～4</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 章，主要讲解</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 入门及其基础</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">使用。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 部分是原理篇，包含第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">5 ～12</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 章，主要讲解如消费原理、负载均衡原理、顺序消</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">息原理等核心的</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 部分。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000">Ⅳ</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">.</span>

## Page 7

<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 部分是进阶篇，包含第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">13 ～16</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 章，主要讲解如消息幂等、双活设计等进阶为架</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">构师必须掌握的内容。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">对于大部分读者，均可以按顺序阅读本书。而对于对</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 已经有一定了解的研</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">发人员，可以跳过基础篇的部分从原理篇开始阅读。同时，读者也可以对感兴趣的话题在</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">进阶篇及原理篇中寻找对应的章节进行阅读。</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">由于笔者水平有限，编撰仓促，书中难免会出现错误，恳请读者的批评、指正。若您</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">有更多宝贵的建议或者意见，也欢迎发送邮件到</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">linjunjie@ apache.org</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">。笔者期待和您交流</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">更多关于</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">、消息中间件、系统设计的话题。</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">首先感谢这些年来笔者公司的同事及领导。通过和他们的交流以及给予的指导，笔者</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">才能有幸深入地了解</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 中优秀的设计原理，同时有机会参与到高并发、高</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">可用的项目设计中。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">其次感谢</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 社区的维护者，正因为他们的努力，一款如此优秀的开源</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">软件才能让更多的人了解、使用。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">最后，笔者要诚挚感谢机械工业出版社的编辑及其他工作人员，有了大家的幕后努力</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">及默默贡献，本书才得以顺利出版。</span>

## Page 8

<span style="font-family:'FZBIAOYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef">前 言</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:13.68pt;color:#00aeef">基</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:13.68pt;color:#00aeef"> </span> <span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:13.68pt;color:#00aeef">础</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:13.68pt;color:#00aeef"> </span> <span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:13.68pt;color:#00aeef">篇</span>

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 1. 4. 1 </span>

## Page 18

<span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff">1</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff">.</span><span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff"> 1</span><span style="font-family:'FZZHUNYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:13.68pt;color:#00aeef"> 为什么高并发系统都绕不开消息中间件</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">为什么需要消息中间件</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">？</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">为什么大型的互联网系统都绕不开消息中间件</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">？</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">相信过往的经历里</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">如架构选型</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">技术面试等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">），</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">你或多或少思考过这个问题</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">其中的答</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">案对于部分读者而言更是信手拈来</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">：</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">如削峰填谷</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">解耦</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">最终一致性等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">但是你是否想过</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">为什么解决互联网场景问题必须要有这些特性</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">？</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">又为什么非得用消息</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">中间件来实现这些特性</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">？</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">下面的例子可以帮助你找到以上问题的答案</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef">1</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef">.</span><span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef"> 1</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef">.</span><span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef"> 1</span><span style="font-family:'FZBIAOYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.74pt;color:#000000"> 初识互联网的架构</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">1.</span><span style="font-family:'FZS3JW--GB1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef"> 一家餐厅的发展历程</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">假设现在有一家很普通的西式快餐厅</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">卖大家很喜欢吃的麦辣鸡腿堡</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">有一天</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">老板请</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">来了一个收银的小姐姐和一个做汉堡的小哥来经营这个餐厅</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">一开始</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">顾客买汉堡包的时候</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">是这样一个流程</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">：</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">顾客点餐后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">收银员就叫汉堡小哥去</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">做指定的汉堡</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">当然了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">做汉堡的时间其实并不会太长</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">因为原材料都是现成的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">但是汉堡</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">小哥总还是得把面包</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">素菜</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">炸鸡腿等合在一起再打包</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">也还是要耗费一点时间的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">上天眷顾</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这家餐厅生意越来越好</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">来光顾的顾客越来越多了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这时候老板就遇到一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">问题</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">：</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">顾客太多</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">都在收银台排长龙了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">小小的门店</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">长龙都排到门外了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">假设做个汉堡需</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">要一分钟</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">排了</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">30</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 个人</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">那么就需要</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">30</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 分钟才能把汉堡交给这些顾客</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">遗憾的是</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">因为队</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">伍太长了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">后面有些顾客看到这么多人</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">都不愿意排了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">直接走了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">所以老板想了一个办法</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">———</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">让收银员收钱后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">就写一个纸条</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">：“</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">24</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 号顾客</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">麦辣鸡腿堡一</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">个</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">然后放到某个地方让汉堡小哥去取</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">然后让顾客先找个地方坐下来等取餐了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">汉堡小哥</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000">2 </span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">.</span>

## Page 19

<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">等忙完了就取一个纸条</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">做对应的汉堡</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">然后送给顾客</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这个方法的确好使</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">长龙的问题终</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">于有了很好的解决方法</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">毕竟收个钱花不了多少时间</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">生意越做越好</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">业务自然也就越来越多</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">老板除了卖汉堡之外</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">又开始打算卖炸薯条和</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">比萨了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">但是这个事情不可能都由汉堡小哥去做呀</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">人家也不愿意啊</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">毕竟只拿一份工资要</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">做三份工作</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">？</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">另一方面</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">培训成本等也是问题</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">所以老板又去请来了薯条小哥和比萨师傅做</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">对应的食品</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这时候轮到收银小姐姐头痛了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">因为卖的东西品种越来越多</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">一个顾客可能同时买汉堡</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">薯条和比萨</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">另一个顾客可能只买汉堡</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">针对前一种情况</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这位小姐姐就需要写三张纸条</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">递到汉堡区</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">薯条区和比萨区</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">她做的事情也越来越多了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">随着老板的业务越来越多</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">还做起了雪糕</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">粥</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">咖啡等生意</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这位小姐姐终于不堪重负</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">离职了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">老板想了想</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">他打算搞一套订单系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">在厨房挂着一个大屏</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">里面显示所有下单的数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">包含哪个客户要吃什么食物</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这样老板新招聘来的小姐姐只需要把客户下的订单录入系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">然后靠屏幕显示给厨房的各个厨师即可</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">于是</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">老板拿出自己的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 祖传</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 编程技术</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">编写一</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">套下单系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">并购买了几个屏幕</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">老板把系统部署后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">就把屏幕挂在不同的工作间里</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">汉堡</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">区</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">雪糕区等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">让不同的厨师看着自己工作区的屏幕来工作</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">之后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">门店运作非常顺畅</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">生意也做得越来越好</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">但是头痛的是</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">系统做得不好</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">业务</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">太多的时候就时不时出现宕机的状况</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">而最惨的是宕机重启后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">还没取餐的订单数据都不再</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">显示了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">导致客户投诉很严重</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">老板最后不得不花钱去找一个专业的公司采购了一套带云存</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">储的系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">2.</span><span style="font-family:'FZS3JW--GB1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef"> 餐厅演进类比互联网架构演进</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">以上这个故事虽然是虚构的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">但实际上和互联网产品的发展阶段十分类似</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">以下一一对</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">应进行说明</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">一开始只经营单一业务</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">收银员下单后需要直接通知汉堡小哥</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">对应着的就是初始版</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">本的系统逻辑通常比较简单</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">系统使用点对点的同步调用</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">生意越来越好</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">导致长龙排到门口</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">新来的客户都不愿意进店了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">对应的是业务带来</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">的流量越来越多</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">耗时导致同步调用达到并发的极限</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">最后无法支撑更多的请求</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">通过写纸条的方式加速收银的速度</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">对应的就是把同步请求异步化</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">增加自身系统的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">吞吐量</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">4</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">老板除了卖汉堡之外</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">还卖起了薯条</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">雪糕</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">比萨等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">导致收银小姐姐工作难度上升</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">而离职</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">对应的则是互联网业务逻辑越来越复杂</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">系统要对接太多外部系统而导致维护</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">开</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">发成本太复杂</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">程序员离职</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZBIAOYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">1</span><span style="font-family:'FZBIAOYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef"> 章</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.73pt;color:#333333">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZBIAOYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#333333"> 综述</span>

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">.</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000">3 </span>

![](./Apache RocketMQ 进阶之路 图解版_15533927 _assets/images/p019_img01.png)

---

## Page 20

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">Apache RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZBIAOYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef"> 进阶之路</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">5</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">老板自己写了一个订单系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">采取屏幕显示的方式降低了收银小姐姐的工作难度</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">对</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">应的就是采取消息的模式</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">做系统的解耦</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">6</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">老板自己写的系统在业务量大的时候出现宕机</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">对应的则是消息系统不堪重负</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">自身</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">支撑不住高并发</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">7</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">老板的系统宕机后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">出现未取餐数据丢失的情况</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">对应的则是消息系统没有高可靠保</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">证</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">导致消息有丢失的可能</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">8</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">老板购买了一套专业的系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">解决宕机和重启后数据丢失的问题</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">对应的则是架构师</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">通过合理的技术选型</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">选择了一套高性能</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">高可靠的消息中间件</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">相信通过这样一个小小的故事</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">你已经了解到消息中间件在其中存在的价值是什么了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">最后回到一开始</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">为什么大型的互联网系统都绕不开消息中间件</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">？”</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 这个问题的答案上</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">展开</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">削峰填谷</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">解耦</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">最终一致性这三点进行独立解读</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef">1</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef">.</span><span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef"> 1</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef">.</span><span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef"> 2</span><span style="font-family:'FZBIAOYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.74pt;color:#000000"> 大型互联网系统遇到的共性挑战</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">1.</span><span style="font-family:'FZS3JW--GB1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef"> 削峰填谷</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这里所谓的削峰填谷</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">其实本质就在于业务系统的处理能力超过了业务的生产速率</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">就</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">像这家餐厅一样</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">客户来的速度总是比厨师烹饪一个食物的时间要快得多</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">所以需要把厨师</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">的工作给异步化</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这听起来挺简单的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">但实际上是要求这个中间的消息系统具备抗流量的能</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">力</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">也就是说</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">消息系统的速度本身应该是支持超高并发的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">否则</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">就像老板自己写的订单</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">系统一样</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">在流量大的时候就宕机了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">2.</span><span style="font-family:'FZS3JW--GB1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef"> 解耦</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">所谓解耦</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">就是当</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">A</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 系统本来需要和</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">B</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">C</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">D</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 多个系统交互的状态中解放出来</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">转向</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">A</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">系统和消息系统交互</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">消息系统自己保证把消息投递给</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">B</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">C</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">D</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 多个系统交互</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这样</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">A</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 终于</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">不需要和</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">B</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">C</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">D</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 进行对接口协议了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">也不需要应付接口变更</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">服务不稳定等问题了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">同</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">时</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这也为</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">A</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">B</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">C</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">D</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 系统本身异构化提供了支持</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">也就是说</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">此时此刻</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">A</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 系统可以使用</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 编写</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">B</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 系统完全可以使用</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 语言编写</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">非常方便</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">3.</span><span style="font-family:'FZS3JW--GB1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef"> 最终一致性</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">所谓最终一致性</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">类似于前文所举的餐厅下单的例子</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">餐厅并不会保证一手收钱一手交</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">货</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">而是先收了你的钱</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">再通过异步的方式保证餐食能就绪</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">让你去取</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">类比在分布式架构中就是</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">A</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 系统的事务需要和</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">B</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 系统的事务保持一致</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">互联网系统通</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">常不使用分布式事务的方式去让两者强一致</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">因为这往往意味着低并发</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">想想餐厅一开始排</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">长龙的例子</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">而是采取消息投递的方式</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">让</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">B</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 系统的事务能最终完成</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000">4 </span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">.</span>

![](./Apache RocketMQ 进阶之路 图解版_15533927 _assets/images/p020_img01.png)



![](./Apache RocketMQ 进阶之路 图解版_15533927 _assets/images/p020_img02.png)

## Page 21

<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这要求消息系统具备两个能力</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">：</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">消息存储的高可靠</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">；</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">消息投递的可靠</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">所谓消息存储的高可靠意味着消息系统重启不会丢失消息</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">甚至消息系统一个节点的磁</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">盘损坏了也不丢失消息</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">所谓消息投递的可靠</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">意味着消费者在消息明确消费完成之前</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">消</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">息系统都不应该标记这个消息是已投递状态或者删除消息</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">4.</span><span style="font-family:'FZS3JW--GB1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef"> 消息中间件如何应对三大挑战</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">以上三点</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">在大型互联网业务的情况下</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">至少会占其一</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">有时甚至三者全占</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">所以消息</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">系统就成为解决这些问题的一个最佳实践了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">可能读者注意到前文一直使用</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 消息系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 这</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">个词</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">而不是用</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">消息中间件</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">因为理论上餐厅的管理者也可以像这个老板一样自己研发一</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">套消息系统去解决类似的问题</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">但事实上</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">要想处理好这三点非常不容易</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">消息中间件就是这类问题通用解决方案的产物</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">不同的消息中间件会有不同的实现原理</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">而大体上都会有类似的特性</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">并且在某个特性上通常有自己闪光的表现</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这就是为什么大型</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">互联网业务架构下</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">都绕不开消息中间件的原因</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">———</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">互联网系统需要用一个消息系统去解决</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">削峰填谷</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">解耦</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">最终一致性的问题</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">而消息中间件就是这个消息系统最佳实践的落地产物</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">作为互联网的架构师或者技术专家</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">往往都是需要选择一款合适业务场景的消息中间件</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">如果没有合适的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">自己研发一套消息系统或者基于开源的消息中间件做定制</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">也是一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">选择</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef">1</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef">.</span><span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef"> 1</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef">.</span><span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef"> 3</span><span style="font-family:'FZBIAOYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.74pt;color:#000000"> 为什么要选择</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:11.74pt;color:#000000">Apache RocketMQ</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">既然要做选型</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">就要了解对应技术对象的重要特性和表现</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">相信到这里</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">读者已经知道</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">了大型互联网系统能从消息中间件中获取最重要的三项收益</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">那么接下来将看看如果将这三</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">个任务交由</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apche RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 来完成的话</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">它的表现如何</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">1. RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZS3JW--GB1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef"> 处理削峰填谷的表现</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">一个消息中间件要能做到削峰填谷</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">需要对其性能有很高的要求</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">因为它需要自身撑得</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">住洪峰的流量</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">否则</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">如果它的性能和业务应用的性能表现差不多的话</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">开发人员何必引入</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">中间件</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">？</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 在性能上有很好的表现</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">按照公开的压测数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">RocketMQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 能拥有媲美</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Kafka</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 的性能发送表现</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">并且在大量分区的场景下性能远超</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Kafka</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">除了性能之外</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">削峰填谷</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">还要求消息中间件有很好的堆积能力</span><s
